They often include: - Synonyms (we did) - Words that can follow a common word (e.g., ____ party) - Words that are part of common phrases (e.g., "___ of the ___") - Words that are types of something (e.g., types of dogs, countries, etc.) - Words that share a letter pattern (like all contain a certain letter, or all have double letters, etc.) - Words that have a certain number of letters. - Words that are palindromes or have other properties.
